## Claim narrowing and non-claims

- This frozen pilot does not include a proposer-by-actor model cross.
- Documented unsupported request fields are omitted and receipted; this does not establish compute matching across model families.
- A model whose decoding seed is documented unsupported is uncalibrated and diagnostic-only unless this exact contract registers and executes a matched A/A null for that model.
- GPT-5.2 Experiment A and C cells are paired on environment seed but reuse no decoded completion and therefore are not fully decoding-matched causal pairs.
- Experiment D memory treatments are a single focal-agent decision-6 prompt pulse followed by a six-step downstream continuation, not a six-step persistent no-memory intervention.
- Experiment C no-error controls are rerun inside Experiment C rather than reused from Experiment B.
- Opus-4.8 has a catalog-attested omission profile but remains zero-dispatch because adding its preregistered capability, preflight, and sentinel cells would violate the frozen cross-model cap under the no-matrix-shrink policy.
- Secondary diagnostic models do not multiply the full A-D matrix.
- The 4-agent by 12-month pilot does not establish full-scale or real-economy validity.
- Legacy, pilot-v1, and interface-debug artifacts are not scientific evidence for this contract.
- `experiment_a` no-go: retain route traceability only.
- `experiment_c` no-go: withdraw or narrow the rule-reliability claim.
- `experiment_d` no-go: do not claim a closed-loop continuation effect.
- `narrative` no-go: no controlled semantic-response claim; never claim real-news understanding.
